SRI  LANKA  INSTITUTE  OF  ARCHITECTS
New registration and renewal of registration of “Chartered architects”, “architects” and “architectural Licentiates” 
for the year 2021/2022 under the architects registration Board, established as per the sri Lanka Institute of architects 
(amendment) act, No. 14 of 1996.
reference is made to the notes appearing on pages 1a, 2a, 3a, 4a and 5a of the Gazette (extraordinary) No.1015/19 
of Friday, the 20 th February, 1998 of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka with regard to the registration of 
persons who are eligible to practice architecture in sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered architects”, “architects” and 
“architectural Licentiates”. The interpretations of the sri Lanka Institute of architects (amendment) act, No. 14 of 1996 in 
the above Gazette Notification will apply in all respects to the list published below.
The architects registration Board of the sri Lanka Institute of architects as per the functions and powers vested 
upon it by the said act. of Parliament, has now prepared the list of the “Chartered architects”, “architects” and “architectural 
Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazetted for the year 2021/2022 (01st February 2021 to 31st january 2022).
The architects registration Board directed me to publish the Names, addresses and registration Numbers 
of the “Chartered architects”, “ architects” and “architectural Licentiates” who have been registered as given below.                                         
This registration expires on 31st january 2022.
 N.w .w. Wijekoon,
 registrar,
 architects registration Board.
sri Lanka Institute of architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha,
Colombo 07,
20
th january 2021.
